
###########################################
#
# Plot Events
#
# ID 7000-8299 is reserved
#
###########################################
# Blackmail									7250-7270
# Drunken Plot Member						7040-7045
#
# Ultimatum event series					8000-8099
# Plot to kill character 					8220-8227
#
# Assassination notification events			8250-8299
#											7700-7999


###########################################
# Blackmail
###########################################
# 7250-7270

# The plot has been leaked
character_event = {
	id = 7250
	desc = "EVTDESC7250"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	only_rulers = yes
	min_age = 16
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_gain_title
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
			has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
			has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
		}
		is_plot_active = no
		num_of_plot_backers = 1
		any_courtier = {
			has_job_title = job_spymaster
			NOT = { is_plot_target_of = PREV }
		}
		top_liege = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
				NOT = { character = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
				any_backed_character = {
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
				NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			liege = {
				any_plot_backer = {
					trait = imbecile
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			liege = {
				any_plot_backer = {
					trait = lunatic
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			liege = { num_of_plot_backers = 2 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.95
			liege = { num_of_plot_backers = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			liege = { num_of_plot_backers = 6 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			liege = { num_of_plot_backers = 8 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7250"
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_realm_lord = {
				limit = {
					primary_title = { higher_tier_than = BARON }
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_liege_of = ROOT }
					NOT = { is_plot_target_of = ROOT }
					any_backed_character = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
					employer = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
					NOT = { opinion = { who = ROOT value = 0 } }
				}
				letter_event = { id = 7255 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail or not
letter_event = {
	id = 7255
	desc = "EVTDESC7255"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7255"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -25 } }
			}
		}
		FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7260 days = 1 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7260" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7255"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = { opinion = { who = FROM value = -50 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail attempt
letter_event = {
	id = 7260
	desc = "EVTDESC7260"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7260"
		wealth = -100
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7265 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7260"
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = { letter_event = { id = 7270 days = 1 } }
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail succeded
letter_event = {
	id = 7265
	desc = "EVTDESC7270"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		treasury = 100
		opinion = {
			modifier = opinion_blackmailed
			who = FROM
			months = 60
		}
	}
}

# Blackmail failed
letter_event = {
	id = 7270
	desc = "EVTDESC7270"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7270"
	}
}


###########################################
# Drunken Plot Member
###########################################
# 7040-7045

# Drunk plot member spills the beans - Non-Murder Plots
character_event = {
	id = 7040
	desc = "EVTDESC7040"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_gain_title
				has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
				has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
				has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
			}
			is_plot_active = no
			NOT = { has_character_flag = event7040 }
			NOT = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = slow
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10.0
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = genius
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = quick
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7040"
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_gain_title
					has_plot = plot_weaken_fellow_vassal
					has_plot = plot_gain_liege_title
					has_plot = plot_gain_fellow_vassal_title
				}
				NOT = { has_character_flag = event7040 }
				NOT = {
					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = revealed_plot
				months = 120
			}
			set_character_flag = event7040
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 7045 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7045
	desc = "EVTDESC7045"
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7045"
		clr_character_flag = event7040
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = scheming_bastard
				who = ROOT
				months = 120
			}
		}
	}
}

# Drunk plot member spills the beans - Murder Plots
character_event = {
	id = 7041
	desc = EVTDESC7040
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			}
			is_plot_active = no
			NOT = { has_character_flag = event7041 }
			NOT = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = drunkard
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			trait = imbecile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			trait = slow
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10.0
			trait = temperate
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			trait = genius
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			trait = quick
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7040
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { has_character_flag = event7041 }
				NOT = {
					plot_target_char = {
						any_known_plotter = {	character = PREVPREV }
					}
				}
			}
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = revealed_plot
				months = 120
			}
			set_character_flag = event7041
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 7046 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Murder plot revealed by drunken backer
character_event = {
	id = 7046
	desc = EVTDESC7045
	picture = GFX_evt_drunk
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA7045
		
		clr_character_flag = event7041
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					any_courtier = {
						has_job_title = job_spymaster
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot_w_message = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				plot_target_char = {
					NOT = {
						any_courtier = {
							has_job_title = job_spymaster
						}
					}
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			save_event_target_as = target_victim
			ROOT = {
				character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
			}
			clear_event_target = target_victim
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - gain a title

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10

			}

				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}		
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8050 }
				any_plot_backer = {
					letter_event = { id = 8070 }
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			plot_target_title = {
				usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = strong
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25

			}

				factor = 1.25

			}

			}

			}

			}

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = { plot_power = 4.0 }
			}

				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Ultimatum - seniority
letter_event = {
	id = 8005
	desc = "EVTDESC8005"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_succ_seniority }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = { 
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_succ_seniority
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0			
				NOT = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power = 
						{
							faction = faction_succ_seniority
							power = 0.5
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = weak
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_succ_seniority }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8076 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8055 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_seniority
					letter_event = { id = 8075 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			faction_succ_seniority = { # The target (title) of the faction
				succession = seniority
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8005"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = strong
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_succ_seniority
						power = 1.5
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_succ_seniority
						power = 1.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_succ_seniority
						power = 2.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_succ_seniority
						power = 3.0
					}
				}
			}	
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_succ_seniority
						power = 4.0
					}
				}
			}				
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.0 } }
				}
				random = {
					chance = 25
					character_event = { id = 45002 days = 120 } # Loyalists flock to the liege's banner
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 8105 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8100" }
			tooltip = {
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_succ_seniority
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.75 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						50 = {
						}
						30 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 0.75 }
						NOT = { faction_power = { faction = faction_succ_seniority power = 1.5 } }
					}
					random_list = {
						75 = {
						}
						5 = {
							character_event = { id = 45000 days = 17 } # A great number of rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
						20 = {
							character_event = { id = 45004 days = 17 } # Rebels flock to the revolter's banner
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Demand accepted - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8061
	desc = "EVTDESC8061"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		supported_claimant = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_very_grateful
				who = ROOT
				years = 10
			}
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
				who = ROOT
				years = 20
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EXCELLENT"
		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		supported_claimant = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					prisoner = yes
					host = { character = FROM  }
				}
				prisoner = no
			}
			ROOT = {
				supported_claimant_title = {
					# If the claimant has the wrong government type, take care of that first.
					if = {
						limit = {
							higher_tier_than = PREVPREV
							holder_scope = {
								OR = {
									is_feudal = yes
									is_tribal = yes
								}
							}
							ROOT = {
								supported_claimant = {
									is_ruler = yes
									OR = {
										is_theocracy = yes
										is_republic = yes
									}
								}
							}
						}
						ROOT = { supported_claimant = { abdicate = yes } }
					}
				
					usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded_and_vassals_no_adj = { target = PREVPREV type = faction_demand }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = 8100
	desc = "EVTDESC8100"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8100"
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		hidden_tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		plot_target_title = {
			reverse_war = {
				target = ROOT
				casus_belli = claim_on_liege_plot
				plot_backers = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8100"
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		prestige = -100
		any_plot_backer = {
			opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_coward
				who = ROOT
				years = 5
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				letter_event = { id = 8120 }
			}
		}
		cancel_plot = plot_gain_title
	}
}

# Demand rejected - Install Claimant
letter_event = {
	id = 8111
	desc = "EVTDESC8100"
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		supported_claimant = {
			reverse_opinion = {
				modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
				who = ROOT
				years = 20
			}
		}
		any_faction_backer = {
			faction = faction_claimant
			supported_claimant = {
				reverse_opinion = {
					modifier = opinion_fought_for_claimant
					who = PREV
					years = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8100"
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				supported_claimant = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			faction_claimant = { # The target (title) of the faction
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = claim_on_liege
					faction = faction_claimant
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					supported_claimant = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			faction_claimant = { # The target (title) of the faction
				reverse_war = {
					target = ROOT
					casus_belli = other_claim_on_liege
					faction = faction_claimant
				}
			}
		}
		
		clr_character_flag = faction_claimant_ultimatum_taken
		
	}
}

### Murder Plot Events ###
#
# 8150-8299

# POISONED WINE - ADULTS ONLY

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisoned Wine
character_event = {
	id = 8150
	desc = "EVTDESC8150"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			prisoner = no
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				trait = on_campaign
			}
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			plot_target_char = { trait = on_campaign }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8150" # The conspirators provide the poison
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8150" # Buy the poison
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8150" # Buy the poison
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC8150" # Hemlock goes well with the Red...
		tooltip_info = learning
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			learning = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 8162 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 8155 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8155" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# A plot backer sees an opportunity - Poisoned Wine
character_event = {
	id = 8151
	desc = EVTDESC8151
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		any_backed_character = {
			OR = {
				has_plot = plot_kill_character
				has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
			}
			plot_power = 0.5
			plot_target_char = {
				age = 16
				prisoner = no
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
			}
			NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
			ROOT = {
				plot_power_contribution = 
				{
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4200
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			plot_target_char = { trait = on_campaign }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				ROOT = {
					plot_power_contribution = 
					{
						plotter = PREV
						power = 0.10
					}
				}
			}
		}

# Poisoned Wine - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8155
	desc = EVTDESC8155
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		prisoner = no
		
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8155" # Drinks the wine
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = temperate
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gluttonous
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = temperate }
						NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8163 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8163 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8156 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8164 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8164 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8157 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8155" # Discovers the poison
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = temperate
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gluttonous
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = temperate }
					NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8165 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8165 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8158 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8166 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8166 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8159 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisoned Wine - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8156
	desc = EVTDESC8156
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8156
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

character_event = {

	desc = "EVTDESC8170"

					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

		modifier = {

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

	}

		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion

# Falling Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 8175
	desc = "EVTDESC8175"
	picture = GFX_evt_feast
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		prisoner = no
		
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8175" # Falls
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8183 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8183 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8176 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8184 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8184 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8177 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8175" # Dodges
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8185 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8185 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8178 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 8186 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 8186 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 8179 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Falling Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 8176
	desc = "EVTDESC8176"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA8176"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

			limit = {
				NOT = { trait = paranoid }
				NOT = { trait = trusting }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				add_trait = paranoid
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				trait = trusting
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				remove_trait = trusting
			}
		}
	}
}

		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				plot_target_title = {
					ROOT = {
						any_vassal = {
							tier = count
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = count
								dejure_liege_title = {
									FROM = {
										plot_target_title = {
											title = PREVPREV
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			plot_target_title = {
				ROOT = {
					random_vassal = {
						limit = {
							tier = count
							any_demesne_title = {
								tier = count
								dejure_liege_title = {
									FROM = {
										plot_target_title = {
											title = PREVPREV
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
						usurp_title = PREVPREV
						hidden_tooltip = {
							character_event = { id = 7515 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 7506 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7505"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				FROM = {
					plot_target_title = {
						ROOT = {
							any_vassal = {
								tier = count
								any_demesne_title = {
									tier = count
									dejure_liege_title = {
										FROM = {
											plot_target_title = {
												title = PREVPREV
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# add effect...
		FROM = {
			plot_target_title = {
				usurp_title = FROM
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = 7517 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #No!
		name = "EVTOPTB7505"
		FROM = {
			letter_event = { id = 7507 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7507" }
		}
	}
}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Archer Ambush
character_event = {
	id = 7700
	desc = "EVTDESC7700"
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			OR = {
				AND = {
					is_ruler = yes
					at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				}
				trait = on_campaign
			}
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
			prisoner = no
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			plot_target_char = { trait = on_campaign }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7700" # The conspirators provide the archers
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7712 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7700" # Hire archers
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { martial = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7712 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7700" # Hire archers
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { martial = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7712 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7700" # Knows good archers
		tooltip_info = martial
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			martial = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7712 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7705 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7705" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { martial = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# Archer Ambush - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7705
	desc = "EVTDESC7705"
	picture = GFX_evt_longbowman
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7705" # Hit by arrows
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = craven
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = craven }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7713 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7713 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7706 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7714 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7714 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7707 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7705" # Avoids arrows
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = craven
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7715 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7715 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7708 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7716 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7716 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7709 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Archer Ambush - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7706
	desc = "EVTDESC7706"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7706"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

	id = 7715
	desc = "EVTDESC7715"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7715"
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion
			tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		}
	}
}

### MANURE EXPLOSION
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Manure Explosion
character_event = {
	id = 7720
	desc = "EVTDESC7720"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				trait = on_campaign
			}
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
			prisoner = no
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			plot_target_char = { trait = on_campaign }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7720" # The conspirators provide the manure
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7722 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7720" # Buy the manure
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7732 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7720" # Buy the manure
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7732 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7720" # Knows farmer
		tooltip_info = stewardship
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			stewardship = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7732 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7725 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7725" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# A plot backer sees an opportunity - Manure Explosion

					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
			character_event = { id = 7730 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { stewardship = 10 }
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {

						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

# Manure Explosion - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7725
	desc = "EVTDESC7725"
	picture = GFX_evt_council
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7725" # Blown up
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7733 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7733 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7726 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7734 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7734 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7727 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7725" # Not blown up
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7735 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7735 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7728 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7736 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7736 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7729 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Manure Explosion - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7726
	desc = "EVTDESC7726"
	picture = GFX_evt_burning_house
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7726"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7740" # The conspirators bribe the maid
		trigger = {

		}

		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 7742 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8152" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7740" # Bribe maid
		trigger = {
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = {
				any_backed_character = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_power = 1.0
				}
			}
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			}
			character_event = { id = 7750 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7740" # Knows maid
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			intrigue = 10
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
		}
		
		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 0.5
			}
			character_event = { id = 7750 days = 3 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8160" }
			set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }

# Infanticide - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7745
	desc = "EVTDESC7745"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7745" # Smothered
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = brave
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gregarious
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = brave }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = gregarious }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7753 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7753 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7746 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7754 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7754 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7747 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7745" # Not smothered
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = brave
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gregarious
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = gregarious }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = brave }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7755 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7755 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7748 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7756 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7756 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7749 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Infanticide - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7746
	desc = "EVTDESC7746"
	picture = GFX_evt_family
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7746"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

character_event = {

	desc = "EVTDESC7760"

	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue

	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

			age = 5
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			prisoner = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution =

				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {

					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7760" # The conspirators get the man inside
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}

			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7765 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7765" } }
	}
	option = {

			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }

					has_plot = plot_kill_character

		}

				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}

					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}

			}
		}

			limit = {

					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}

		random_backed_character = {
			limit = {

# Prison Break - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7765
	desc = "EVTDESC7765"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7765" # Tries to escape
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = craven
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = craven }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7773 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7773 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7766 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7774 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7774 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7767 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7765" # Does not try to escape
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = craven
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7775 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7775 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7768 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7776 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7776 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7769 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Prison Break - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7766
	desc = "EVTDESC7766"
	picture = GFX_evt_into_the_dungeon
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7766"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

character_event = {
	id = 7780
	desc = "EVTDESC7780"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			trait = incapable
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution =

			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}

				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

			factor = 0.33

					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7780" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7782 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7785 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7785" } }

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7780" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }

# Bathtub Drowning - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7785
	desc = "EVTDESC7785"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7785" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = strong
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = weak
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = weak }
						NOT = { trait = strong }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7793 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7793 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7786 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7794 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7794 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7787 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7785" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = strong
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = weak
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = weak }
					NOT = { trait = strong }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7795 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7795 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7788 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7796 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7796 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7789 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Bathtub Drowning - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7786
	desc = "EVTDESC7786"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7786"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

character_event = {
	id = 7800
	desc = "EVTDESC7800"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no

			age = 5

			NOT = { trait = incapable }

					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		trigger = {

			plot_target_char = {
				age = 5
				NOT = { age = 16 }
				NOT = { trait = incapable }
				NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
				prisoner = no
			}
			NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
			ROOT = {
				plot_power_contribution = 
				{
					plotter = PREV
					power = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3600
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {

# Boating Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7805
	desc = "EVTDESC7805"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7805" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7813 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7813 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7806 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7814 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7814 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7807 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7805" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = strong
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = weak
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = weak }
					NOT = { trait = strong }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7815 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7815 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7808 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7816 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7816 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7809 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Boating Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7806
	desc = "EVTDESC7806"
	picture = GFX_evt_kraken
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7806"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

				}

					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

### POISONOUS SNAKE
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Poisonous Snake
character_event = {
	id = 7820
	desc = "EVTDESC7820"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				trait = on_campaign
			}
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			plot_target_char = { trait = on_campaign }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution =

				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			plot_power_contribution =

				power = 0.70

		}

			}
		}

			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7820" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7822 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7825 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7825" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7820" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7832 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7825 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7825" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7820" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { learning = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {

				character_event = { id = 7832 days = 1 }
			}
		}

	}
	option = {

		}

# Poisonous Snake - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7825
	desc = "EVTDESC7825"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7825" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = craven
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = slothful
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = craven }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = slothful }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7833 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7826 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7834 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7827 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7825" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = craven
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = slothful
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = craven }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = slothful }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7835 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7835 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7828 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7836 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7836 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7829 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Poisonous Snake - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7826
	desc = "EVTDESC7826"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadow
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7826"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Poisonous Snake - Notification: Failure, and discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7835
	desc = "EVTDESC7835"
	picture = GFX_evt_shadowy_cabal
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		# Set opinions vs the bungling killer
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_murder_attempt
				months = 120
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = opinion_dishonorable
				months = 60
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { FROM = { employer = { character = ROOT } } }
			}
			FROM = { 
				employer = {
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_dishonorable
						months = 60
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			any_dynasty_member = {
				limit = {
					is_alive = yes
					NOT = { character = ROOT }
				}
				opinion = {
					who = ROOT
					modifier = opinion_dishonorable
					months = 60
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7835"
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion
			tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		}
	}
}

### BALCONY PLUMMET
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Balcony Plummet
character_event = {
	id = 7840
	desc = "EVTDESC7840"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				trait = on_campaign
			}
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {

		}

				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7840" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7842 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7840" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7852 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7840" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7852 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7840" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7852 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7845 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7845" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# Balcony Plummet - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7845
	desc = "EVTDESC7845"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7845" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7853 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7853 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7846 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7854 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7854 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7847 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7845" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7855 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7855 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7848 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7856 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7856 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7849 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Balcony Plummet - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7846
	desc = "EVTDESC7846"
	picture = GFX_evt_castle_construction
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7846"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

### HUNTING ACCIDENT - CHILDREN ONLY
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Hunting Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7860
	desc = "EVTDESC7860"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 5
			NOT = { age = 16 }
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 3600
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
