# Hunting Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7865
	desc = "EVTDESC7865"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7865" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gregarious
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = gregarious }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7873 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7873 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7866 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7874 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7874 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7867 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7865" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gregarious
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = gregarious }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7875 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7875 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7868 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7876 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7876 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7869 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Hunting Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7866
	desc = "EVTDESC7866"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7866"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Hunting Accident - Notification: Failure, and discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7875
	desc = "EVTDESC7875"
	picture = GFX_evt_hunt
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7875"
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion
			tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		}

# The plotter sees an opportunity - Disguised Highwaymen
character_event = {
	id = 7880
	desc = "EVTDESC7880"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				trait = on_campaign
			}
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			plot_target_char = { trait = on_campaign }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7880" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7882 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7885 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7885" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7880" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7892 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7885 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7885" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7880" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7892 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7885 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7885" } }

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}

# Disguised Highwaymen - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7885
	desc = "EVTDESC7885"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7885" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7893 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7893 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7886 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7894 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7894 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7887 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7885" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7895 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7895 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7888 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7896 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7896 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7889 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Disguised Highwaymen - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7886
	desc = "EVTDESC7886"
	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7886"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

	picture = GFX_evt_bandits
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		character_event = { id = 11 } # Consequences of discovery
		clear_event_target = target_victim
		
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			reveal_plot = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7895"
		if = {
			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion
			tooltip = { reveal_plot = yes }
		}
	}
}

### CARRIAGE ACCIDENT
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Carriage Accident
character_event = {
	id = 7900
	desc = "EVTDESC7900"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			OR = {
				at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
				trait = on_campaign
			}
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 8400
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			plot_target_char = { trait = on_campaign }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7900" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7902 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7900" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7900" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7900" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7912 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7905 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7905" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# Carriage Accident - Plot backer requests funds
character_event = {
	id = 7902
	desc = "EVTDESC7902"
	picture = GFX_evt_spymaster
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7902"
		transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				from = ROOT
				to = FROM
				value = 1.0
		}
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7903 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8153" } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8152"
		FROM = { character_event = { id = 7904 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP8154" } }
	}
}

	id = 7904

		name = "EVTOPTA8154" # Pay for it myself

		FROM = { clr_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
	}

# Carriage Accident - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7905
	desc = "EVTDESC7905"
	picture = GFX_evt_carriage
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7905" # Drowns
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = paranoid
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = diligent
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = trusting
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = diligent }
						NOT = { trait = paranoid }
						NOT = { trait = trusting }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7913 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7913 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7906 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7914 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7914 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7907 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7905" # Does not drown
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = paranoid
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = diligent
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = trusting
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = diligent }
					NOT = { trait = paranoid }
					NOT = { trait = trusting }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7915 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7915 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7908 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7916 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7916 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7909 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Carriage Accident - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7906
	desc = "EVTDESC7906"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7906"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Carriage Accident - Dies, murderer NOT discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7907
	desc = "EVTDESC7906"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7907"
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_unknown
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder_unknown

			limit = { 
				plot_target_char = {
					character = FROM
				}
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse

		}

### DECADENT DEBAUCHERY
# The plotter sees an opportunity - Decadent Debauchery
character_event = {
	id = 7950
	desc = "EVTDESC7950"
	picture = GFX_evt_whispers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	capable_only = yes
	prisoner = no
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_plot = plot_kill_character
			has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
		}
		plot_target_char = {
			age = 16
			NOT = { trait = incapable }
			prisoner = no
			at_location = ROOT # The Plot Head needs to be at the target's location to get a chance
			NOT = { trait = in_hiding }
			trait = decadent
			dynasty = ROOT
		}
		NOT = { has_character_flag = murder_in_motion }
		plot_power_contribution = 
		{
			plotter = ROOT
			power = 0.025
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 7300
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.10
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.20
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.30
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.40
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.50
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.60
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.70
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.80
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 0.90
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			plot_power_contribution = 
			{
				plotter = ROOT
				power = 1.5
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.0
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 1.5
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			any_backed_character = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_power = 2.0
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7950" # The conspirators bribe the servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 1.0
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
					character_event = { id = 7952 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7955 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7955" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7950" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			NOT = { plot_power = 0.5 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -1.0
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7962 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7955 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7955" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7950" # Bribe servants
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
		}
		scaled_wealth = -0.5
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7962 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7955 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7955" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC7950" # Replace with own servants
		tooltip_info = intrigue
		trigger = {
			plot_power = 0.5
			intrigue = 10
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_plot_backer = {
				character_event = { id = 7962 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		set_character_flag = murder_in_motion
		plot_target_char = { character_event = { id = 7955 days = 30 tooltip = "EVTTOOLTIP7955" } }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTD8150" # I cannot afford this
		trigger = {
			ai = no
			NOT = { intrigue = 10 }
			NOT = { plot_power = 1.0 }
		}
	}
}

# Decadent Debauchery - the murder attempt
character_event = {
	id = 7955
	desc = "EVTDESC7955"
	picture = GFX_evt_jugglers
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	hide_from = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		save_event_target_as = target_victim
	}
	
	trigger = {
		# Is the plot still in motion?
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
			FROMFROM = {
				OR = {
					has_plot = plot_kill_character
					has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
				}
				plot_target_char = {
					character = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7955" # Dies
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					trait = slothful
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = proud
					random = 33
				}
				AND = {
					trait = hedonist
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = gluttonous
					random = 50
				}
				AND = {
					trait = drunkard
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					trait = lustful
					random = 90
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { trait = drunkard }
					NOT = { trait = hedonist }
					NOT = { trait = lustful }
					NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
					NOT = { trait = slothful }
					NOT = { trait = proud }
					random = 75
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				25 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7963 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7963 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7956 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer discovered
				}
				75 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7964 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7964 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7957 days = 1 } # Dies, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB7955" # Does not die
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						trait = slothful
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = proud
						random = 33
					}
					AND = {
						trait = hedonist
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = gluttonous
						random = 50
					}
					AND = {
						trait = drunkard
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						trait = lustful
						random = 90
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { trait = drunkard }
						NOT = { trait = hedonist }
						NOT = { trait = lustful }
						NOT = { trait = gluttonous }
						NOT = { trait = slothful }
						NOT = { trait = proud }
						random = 75
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7965 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7965 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7958 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer discovered
				}
				50 = {
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = { character_event = { id = 7966 days = 1 } }
						FROMFROM = { character_event = { id = 7966 days = 1 } }
					}
					character_event = { id = 7959 days = 1 } # Lives, murderer unknown
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Decadent Debauchery - Dies, murderer(s) discovered
character_event = {
	id = 7956
	desc = "EVTDESC7956"
	picture = GFX_evt_death
	border = GFX_event_normal_frame_intrigue
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA7956"
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROMFROMFROM = {
					OR = {
						has_plot = plot_kill_character
						has_plot = plot_kill_spouse
					}
					plot_target_char = {
						character = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROMFROM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_alive = yes
			}
			death = {
				death_reason = death_murder
				killer = FROMFROM
			}
		}
	}
	
}

# Ultimatum - antiking
letter_event = {
	id = 8200
	desc = EVTDESC8200
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		FROM = { in_faction = faction_antiking }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		FROM = {
			diplomatic_immunity = yes 
			any_faction_backer = {
				faction = faction_antiking
				diplomatic_immunity = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVTOPTA8000
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					FROM = {
						faction_power = 
						{
							faction = faction_antiking
							power = 1.0
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = weak
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = craven
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = humble
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = kind
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = charitable
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = patient
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = content
			}
		}
		
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_vassal = {
				limit = {
					ai = no
					NOT = { in_faction = faction_antiking }
				}
				character_event = { id = 8202 }
			}
			FROM = {
				letter_event = { id = 8203 }
				any_faction_backer = {
					faction = faction_antiking
					letter_event = { id = 8201 }
					diplomatic_immunity = no
				}
				diplomatic_immunity = no
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			religion_authority = {
				modifier = deposed_antipope
				years = 50
			}
			faction_antiking = { # The target (title) of the faction
				if = {
					limit = { has_law = investiture_law_1 }
					add_law_w_cooldown = investiture_law_0
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						religion = catholic
					}
					k_papal_state = {
						holder_scope = {
							opinion = {
								who = PREVPREV
								modifier = opinion_deposed_antipope
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						religion = ursuline
					}
					k_ursuline = {
						holder_scope = {
							opinion = {
								who = PREVPREV
								modifier = opinion_deposed_antipope
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			rightful_religious_head_scope = {
				remove_claim = k_papal_state
				remove_claim = k_ursuline
			}
		}
		
		primary_title = {
			usurp_title = FROM
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB8000"
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = strong
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = brave
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = proud
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = envious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = greedy
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = wroth
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				trait = ambitious
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_antiking
						power = 1.5
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_antiking
						power = 1.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				FROM = {
					faction_power = 
					{
						faction = faction_antiking
						power = 2.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {

					{
						faction = faction_antiking
						power = 3.0
					}

			}
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {

				}
				random = {
					chance = 25

				}

		}
		FROM = {

						}

						}

					}

						}

						}
					}
